<li>Dōnggǎng Music Fountain</li>
<li>Fùjiāzhuāng</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Jinzhou_District_and_Development_Zone_.28in_the_northern_suburbs.29">Jinzhou District and Development Zone (in the northern suburbs)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Dalian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Jinzhou District and Development Zone (in the northern suburbs)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Dahei_Mountain" title="Dahei Mountain">Dahei Mountain</a></li>
<li>Jinshitan National Holiday Resort and the <a href="/wiki/Dalian_Discovery_Kingdom" title="Dalian Discovery Kingdom">Discoveryland</a> (pinyin: <i><span lang="zh-Latn-pinyin">jinshitan l=Golden Pebble Beach</span></i>) is composed of eastern peninsula, western peninsula, open ground between two peninsulas and the ten-mile Golden Coast beach. Major sightseeing points include, Golden Pebble Waxworks Museum, Geological Museum, Coastal National Geopark, International Vehicle Campsite, Tang Dynasty Hot Spring Resort, Golden Rock Park, Wanfuding Park, <a href="/wiki/China" title="China">China</a> Martial Arts Hall, <a href="/wiki/Dalian_Discovery_Kingdom" title="Dalian Discovery Kingdom">Discoveryland Theme Park</a>, <a href="/wiki/Chairman_Mao_badge" title="Chairman Mao badge">Mao Zedong Badge</a> Exhibition Hall, Model Movie &amp; TV Art Center, Golden Pebble Hunting Club, Golden Pebble Equestrianism Base, Golden Pebble International Convention Center &amp; Resort, Golden Pebble Golf Club, and Golden Gulf Golf Course. Several themed events, such as Dalian International Beach Carnival, International Winter Swimming Festival and Grape Festival, take place in Jinshitan annually.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-62"><a href="#cite_note-62">[62]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dd>The <a href="/wiki/Dalian_Discovery_Kingdom" title="Dalian Discovery Kingdom">Discoveryland Theme Park</a> (<span lang="zh-Hans">发现王国</span>, also translated as "the Discovery Kingdom") was built in 2006 and covers an area of 470,000 square miles (1,217,294 square kilometres).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-dis_63-0"><a href="#cite_note-dis-63">[63]</a></sup> It was designed by <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Romero_Petrilli_VanRell_Associates&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Romero Petrilli VanRell Associates (page does not exist)">Romero Petrilli VanRell Associates</a> who participated in the design of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Disney_theme_park" title="Disney theme park">Disney theme park</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-dis_63-1"><a href="#cite_note-dis-63">[63]</a></sup></dd>
</dl>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="L.C3.BCshunkou_District_.28in_the_southwestern_suburbs.29">Lüshunkou District (in the southwestern suburbs)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Dalian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Lüshunkou District (in the southwestern suburbs)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Lushun_Museum" title="Lushun Museum">Lüshun Museum</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lushun_Railway_Station" title="Lushun Railway Station">Lüshun Railway Station</a></li>
<li>East Jīguàn Mountain (<span lang="zh">东鸡冠山</span>), <a href="/wiki/203_Hill" title="203 Hill">203 Hill</a> and <a href="/wiki/Shuishiying" title="Shuishiying">Shuishiying</a> Meeting Place</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dd>The fiercest battle site and the signing site of the ceasefire treaty, of the Battle of Lüshun during the <a href="/wiki/Russo-Japanese_War" title="Russo-Japanese War">Russo-Japanese War</a> (1904–05).</dd>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Japanese and Russian Prison Site Museum in Lüshun</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dd>The prison was built by Russians in 1902 and later expanded by the Japanese. During <a href="/wiki/World_War_II" title="World War II">World War II</a>, the prison was used to detain people of various nationalities who were against Japanese invasion. <a href="/wiki/An_Jung-geun" title="An Jung-geun">An Jung-geun</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Korean_independence_movement" title="Korean independence movement">Korean independence activist</a> who assassinated <a href="/wiki/It%C5%8D_Hirobumi" title="Itō Hirobumi">Itō Hirobumi</a>, was imprisoned and killed there.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-64"><a href="#cite_note-64">[64]</a></sup></dd>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Lüshun Snake Museum, and Lüshun Bird Port and Snake Island Reservation</li>
<li>Hengshan Temple and <a href="/wiki/Longwangtang_Cherry_Blossom_Park" title="Longwangtang Cherry Blossom Park">Longwangtang Cherry Blossom Park</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dd>Héngshān Temple (<span lang="zh">横山寺</span>) is near Lóngwángtáng Reservoir (<span lang="zh">龙王塘水库</span>). The temple dates back to the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Han_Dynasty" title="Han Dynasty">Han Dynasty</a>, and was rebuilt in 2003.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-65"><a href="#cite_note-65">[65]</a></sup></dd>
</dl>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Hengshan_Temple.JPG"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3456" data-file-width="5184" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6f/Hengshan_Temple.JPG/220px-Hengshan_Temple.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6f/Hengshan_Temple.JPG/330px-Hengshan_Temple.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6f/Hengshan_Temple.JPG/440px-Hengshan_Temple.JPG 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Hengshan_Temple.JPG" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Hengshan Temple in <a href="/wiki/L%C3%BCshunkou_District" title="Lüshunkou District">Lüshunkou District</a></div>
</div>
</div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Three_Northern_District_and_Cities_of_Greater_Dalian">Three Northern District and Cities of Greater Dalian</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Dalian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Three Northern District and Cities of Greater Dalian">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>Ānbō Hotspring and Ski Course (<span lang="zh">安波温泉滑雪场</span>), in <a href="/wiki/Pulandian_District" title="Pulandian District">Pulandian District</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Changxing_Island_(Dalian)" title="Changxing Island (Dalian)">Changxing Island</a> International Golf Course, in <a href="/wiki/Wafangdian" title="Wafangdian">Wafangdian</a></li>
<li>Bīngyùgōu (<span lang="zh">冰峪沟</span>) Scenic Area and Bùyún Mountain Hot Spring (<span lang="zh">步云山温泉</span>), in <a href="/wiki/Zhuanghe" title="Zhuanghe">Zhuanghe</a></li>
<li>Islands of <a href="/wiki/Changhai_County" title="Changhai County">Changhai County</a></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Hot_Spring_and_Ski_Resorts">Hot Spring and Ski Resorts</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Dalian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Hot Spring and Ski Resorts">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>There are various hot spring hotels in Dalian. Notable ones include, Laotieshan Hot Spring Hotel in Lüshun, Tang Dynasty Hot Spring Resort in Jinshitan, Minghu Hot Spring Hotel in Wafangdian City, Chengyuan Hot Spring Villa in Ganjingzi District, and Tianmu Hot Spring Hotel in Lüshun.</p>
<p>Skiing has become increasingly popular in Dalian. Famous ski resorts are, Linhai Ski Resort in Ganjingzi District, Anbo Ski Resort in Pulandian District, Minghu Ski Resort &amp; Minghu International Skiing Holiday Village in Wafangdian City, and Dalian Happy Snow World in Ganjingzi District near the airport.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-66"><a href="#cite_note-66">[66]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Transportation">Transportation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Dalian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Transportation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Dalian_Metro_Line_2.JPG"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2448" data-file-width="3264" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7e/Dalian_Metro_Line_2.JPG/220px-Dalian_Metro_Line_2.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7e/Dalian_Metro_Line_2.JPG/330px-Dalian_Metro_Line_2.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7e/Dalian_Metro_Line_2.JPG/440px-Dalian_Metro_Line_2.JPG 2x" width="220"/></a>

<a href="/wiki/Dalian_Metro" title="Dalian Metro">Dalian Metro</a>, <a href="/wiki/Line_2,_Dalian_Metro" title="Line 2, Dalian Metro">Line 2</a></div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="thumb tleft">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Dalian_Liaoning_China_Historical-Tramway-01.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2592" data-file-width="3888" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/45/Dalian_Liaoning_China_Historical-Tramway-01.jpg/220px-Dalian_Liaoning_China_Historical-Tramway-01.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/45/Dalian_Liaoning_China_Historical-Tramway-01.jpg/330px-Dalian_Liaoning_China_Historical-Tramway-01.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/45/Dalian_Liaoning_China_Historical-Tramway-01.jpg/440px-Dalian_Liaoning_China_Historical-Tramway-01.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>

Dalian historical tramway. Its use is still preserved to date in limited area in the city</div>
</div>
</div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Local_transportation">Local transportation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Dalian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Local transportation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Not many people ride bicycles in Dalian because of the hilly roads. Dalian is also one of the many cities in China where there are few motorcycles, because motorcycle riding on most roads is banned by law.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-67"><a href="#cite_note-67">[67]</a></sup> The city has a comprehensive bus system and an efficient metro system. As of November 2015, the <a href="/wiki/Dalian_Metro" title="Dalian Metro">Dalian Metro</a> consists of the underground <a href="/wiki/Line_1,_Dalian_Metro" title="Line 1, Dalian Metro">Line 1</a>, <a href="/wiki/Line_2,_Dalian_Metro" title="Line 2, Dalian Metro">Line 2</a>, and the overground <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Line_R2,_Dalian_Metro" title="Line R2, Dalian Metro">Line R2</a> and <a href="/wiki/Line_3,_Dalian_Metro" title="Line 3, Dalian Metro">Line 3</a>. New lines and expansion of the metro system are under way. The <a href="/wiki/Trams_in_Dalian" title="Trams in Dalian">Dalian Tram</a> system is the second oldest in China. Most of the public transportation in the city can be accessed using the Mingzhu <a href="/wiki/Smart_card" title="Smart card">IC Card</a> (<span lang="zh">明珠卡</span>).</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Domestic_and_international">Domestic and international</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Dalian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Domestic and international">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Dalian_North_Railway_Station_Interior.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1920" data-file-width="2560" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/Dalian_North_Railway_Station_Interior.jpg/220px-Dalian_North_Railway_Station_Interior.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/Dalian_North_Railway_Station_Interior.jpg/330px-Dalian_North_Railway_Station_Interior.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/Dalian_North_Railway_Station_Interior.jpg/440px-Dalian_North_Railway_Station_Interior.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Dalian_North_Railway_Station_Interior.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Internal view of <a href="/wiki/Dalian_North_Railway_Station" title="Dalian North Railway Station">Dalian North Railway Station</a></div>
</div>
</div>
<p>In 2005 Dalian expanded the international airport, <a href="/wiki/Dalian_Zhoushuizi_International_Airport" title="Dalian Zhoushuizi International Airport">Dalian Zhoushuizi International Airport</a>, with direct flights to the most major cities in China, and to some cities in <a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japan</a>, <a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korea</a> and <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>. In 2014, the airport was the <a href="/wiki/List_of_the_busiest_airports_in_China" title="List of the busiest airports in China">20th busiest</a> airport in China with 13,551,223 passengers.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-68"><a href="#cite_note-68">[68]</a></sup> The airport is the hub of <a href="/wiki/Dalian_Airlines" title="Dalian Airlines">Dalian Airlines</a>.</p>
<p>The city's location means that train trips to most Chinese cities outside China's northeastern region require changing trains in <a href="/wiki/Beijing" title="Beijing">Beijing</a> or <a href="/wiki/Shanghai" title="Shanghai">Shanghai</a>. With the <a href="/wiki/High-speed_rail_in_China" title="High-speed rail in China">high-speed rail system</a>, trips from Dalian to <a href="/wiki/Shenyang" title="Shenyang">Shenyang</a> can be completed in 1.5 hours, to <a href="/wiki/Changchun" title="Changchun">Changchun</a> 2.5 hours and to <a href="/wiki/Harbin" title="Harbin">Harbin</a> 3.5 hours. The city has two railway stations, namely <a href="/wiki/Dalian_Railway_Station" title="Dalian Railway Station">Dalian Railway Station</a> and <a href="/wiki/Dalian_North_Railway_Station" title="Dalian North Railway Station">Dalian North Railway Station</a> (<a href="/wiki/International_Air_Transport_Association_airport_code" title="International Air Transport Association airport code">IATA</a>: <b>DBL</b>)<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (September 2015)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup>, the latter being part of the <a href="/wiki/Harbin%E2%80%93Dalian_High-Speed_Railway" title="Harbin–Dalian High-Speed Railway">Harbin–Dalian High-Speed Railway</a>.</p>
<p>In addition to local and express bus services to Beijing and other areas in the northeast, Dalian is connected by passenger ship service to neighbouring coastal cities, including <a href="/wiki/Tianjin" title="Tianjin">Tianjin</a>, <a href="/wiki/Yantai" title="Yantai">Yantai</a>, <a href="/wiki/Weihai" title="Weihai">Weihai</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Penglai_City" title="Penglai City">Penglai</a> and <a href="/wiki/Dongying" title="Dongying">Dongying</a>, as well as <a href="/wiki/Incheon" title="Incheon">Incheon</a>, <a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korea</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-port_43-2"><a href="#cite_note-port-43">[43]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Culture">Culture</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Dalian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Culture">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Dalian_Peking_Opera_House.JPG"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3456" data-file-width="5184" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/64/Dalian_Peking_Opera_House.JPG/220px-Dalian_Peking_Opera_House.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/64/Dalian_Peking_Opera_House.JPG/330px-Dalian_Peking_Opera_House.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/64/Dalian_Peking_Opera_House.JPG/440px-Dalian_Peking_Opera_House.JPG 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Dalian_Peking_Opera_House.JPG" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Dalian <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Peking_Opera" title="Peking Opera">Peking Opera</a> House</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>In 2006, Dalian was selected as the most liveable city in China according to <i><a href="/wiki/China_Daily" title="China Daily">China Daily</a></i>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-69"><a href="#cite_note-69">[69]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Dalian_dialect">Dalian dialect</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Dalian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Dalian dialect">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Dalian_dialect" title="Dalian dialect">Dalian dialect</a></div>
<p><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Standard_Mandarin" title="Standard Mandarin">Standard Mandarin</a> is usually spoken in Dalian because it is a city with people from various locations. But native Dalianites use a <a href="/wiki/Dalian_dialect" title="Dalian dialect">Dalian dialect</a>, which belongs to the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Jiao_Liao_Mandarin" title="Jiao Liao Mandarin">Jiao Liao Mandarin</a> subgroup spoken in parts of <a href="/wiki/Shandong" title="Shandong">Shandong</a> and <a href="/wiki/Liaoning" title="Liaoning">Liaoning</a> provinces. Most of the original Dalianites were farmers and fishermen who had come from Shandong Province in a large population move, the <i><a href="/wiki/Chuang_Guandong" title="Chuang Guandong">Chuang Guandong</a></i>, during which era Dalian was occupied by the Japanese as the <a href="/wiki/Kwantung_Leased_Territory" title="Kwantung Leased Territory">Kwantung Leased Territory</a>. The Dalian dialect incorporates a few <a href="/wiki/Loanword" title="Loanword">loanwords</a> from <a href="/wiki/Japanese_language" title="Japanese language">Japanese</a> and <a href="/wiki/Russian_language" title="Russian language">Russian</a> (very rare in Chinese), reflecting the history of foreign occupation.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-70"><a href="#cite_note-70">[70]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Cuisine">Cuisine</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Dalian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Cuisine">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tmulti tleft">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:169px;max-width:169px">
<div class="tsingle" style="margin:1px;width:167px;max-width:167px">
<div class="thumbimage"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Salted_fish_Dalian.JPG"><img alt="" data-file-height="3672" data-file-width="4896" height="124" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/53/Salted_fish_Dalian.JPG/165px-Salted_fish_Dalian.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/53/Salted_fish_Dalian.JPG/248px-Salted_fish_Dalian.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/53/Salted_fish_Dalian.JPG/330px-Salted_fish_Dalian.JPG 2x" width="165"/></a></div>
<div class="thumbcaption" style="clear:left">Salted fish with corn cake</div>
</div>
<div class="tsingle" style="margin:1px;width:167px;max-width:167px">
<div class="thumbimage"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Dalian_Menzi.JPG"><img alt="" data-file-height="3462" data-file-width="4896" height="117" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Dalian_Menzi.JPG/165px-Dalian_Menzi.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Dalian_Menzi.JPG/248px-Dalian_Menzi.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Dalian_Menzi.JPG/330px-Dalian_Menzi.JPG 2x" width="165"/></a></div>
<div class="thumbcaption" style="clear:left">Dalian Menzi, a popular local snack</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:%E5%A4%A7%E8%BF%9E%E4%B8%AD%E5%B1%B1%E7%BE%8E%E6%9C%AF%E9%A6%86.JPG"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3672" data-file-width="4896" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/54/%E5%A4%A7%E8%BF%9E%E4%B8%AD%E5%B1%B1%E7%BE%8E%E6%9C%AF%E9%A6%86.JPG/220px-%E5%A4%A7%E8%BF%9E%E4%B8%AD%E5%B1%B1%E7%BE%8E%E6%9C%AF%E9%A6%86.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/54/%E5%A4%A7%E8%BF%9E%E4%B8%AD%E5%B1%B1%E7%BE%8E%E6%9C%AF%E9%A6%86.JPG/330px-%E5%A4%A7%E8%BF%9E%E4%B8%AD%E5%B1%B1%E7%BE%8E%E6%9C%AF%E9%A6%86.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/54/%E5%A4%A7%E8%BF%9E%E4%B8%AD%E5%B1%B1%E7%BE%8E%E6%9C%AF%E9%A6%86.JPG/440px-%E5%A4%A7%E8%BF%9E%E4%B8%AD%E5%B1%B1%E7%BE%8E%E6%9C%AF%E9%A6%86.JPG 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:%E5%A4%A7%E8%BF%9E%E4%B8%AD%E5%B1%B1%E7%BE%8E%E6%9C%AF%E9%A6%86.JPG" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Zhongshan Art Museum</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Dalian cuisine is a branch of <a href="/wiki/Shandong_cuisine" title="Shandong cuisine">Shandong cuisine</a>, with influence from <a href="/wiki/Northeastern_Chinese_cuisine" title="Northeastern Chinese cuisine">Northeastern Chinese cuisine</a>, and is widely known for its unique style of seafood dishes. The variety of seafood in Dalian includes fish, prawns, clams, crabs, scallops, sea urchins, oysters, sea cucumbers, mussels, lobsters, <a href="/wiki/Conch" title="Conch">conches</a>, <a href="/wiki/Abalone" title="Abalone">abalone</a>, <a href="/wiki/Algae" title="Algae">algae</a>, <a href="/wiki/Razor_shell" title="Razor shell">razor clams</a>, <a href="/wiki/Urechis_unicinctus" title="Urechis unicinctus">urechis unicinctus</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mantis_shrimps" title="Mantis shrimps">mantis shrimps</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jellyfish" title="Jellyfish">jellyfish</a> and so on.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (January 2015)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></p>
<p>Colorful snowflake scallops (<span lang="zh-Hans">五彩雪花扇贝</span>) is a local seafood dish, where egg white is made into snowflake-shape to embrace the scallops, with seasonal greens, carrot and hot pepper cut into small pieces as decorations on top.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-71"><a href="#cite_note-71">[71]</a></sup></p>
<p>Another popular local dish is Salted fish with corn cake (<span lang="zh-Hans">咸鱼饼子</span>), where steamed or fried corn cake is served with fried salted fish. Legend goes that, in the old days fishermen going out fishing in the morning couldn't return home to have lunch, so they baked fresh fish to eat with corn cakes, and the habit passed down from generation to generation and eventually became a famous food among local people.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-dine_72-0"><a href="#cite_note-dine-72">[72]</a></sup></p>
<p>Dalian Menzi (<span lang="zh-Hans">焖子</span>) is a traditional local snack. A protein-rich starch paste coagulated from an extract of potatoes is cut into pieces and fried on a pan to create a crisp cover. A mixed seasoning of smashed garlic, sesame, and sauces is added on eating.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-dine_72-1"><a href="#cite_note-dine-72">[72]</a></sup></p>
<p>Other popular local specialties include Dalian-style grilled squid, seafood noodles, roast full prawns, salt baked conches, lantern-shaped steamed abalone, and so on.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-73"><a href="#cite_note-73">[73]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sports">Sports</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Dalian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Sports">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:%E4%B8%AD%E5%8D%8E%E6%AD%A6%E9%A6%86.JPG"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3672" data-file-width="4896" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0e/%E4%B8%AD%E5%8D%8E%E6%AD%A6%E9%A6%86.JPG/220px-%E4%B8%AD%E5%8D%8E%E6%AD%A6%E9%A6%86.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0e/%E4%B8%AD%E5%8D%8E%E6%AD%A6%E9%A6%86.JPG/330px-%E4%B8%AD%E5%8D%8E%E6%AD%A6%E9%A6%86.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0e/%E4%B8%AD%E5%8D%8E%E6%AD%A6%E9%A6%86.JPG/440px-%E4%B8%AD%E5%8D%8E%E6%AD%A6%E9%A6%86.JPG 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:%E4%B8%AD%E5%8D%8E%E6%AD%A6%E9%A6%86.JPG" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
China Martial Arts Hall, at Jinshitan National Holiday Resort</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Sports play a big role in the local culture. Dalian's former <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">association football</a> club, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Dalian_Shide" title="Dalian Shide">Dalian Shide</a> (formerly known as Dalian Wanda as the club was originally sponsored by the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Dalian_Wanda_Group" title="Dalian Wanda Group">Dalian Wanda Group</a>), achieved a total of <a href="/wiki/Chinese_Super_League#Most_successful_clubs" title="Chinese Super League">eight titles</a> from China's top-tier football league, the <a href="/wiki/Chinese_Jia-A_League" title="Chinese Jia-A League">Chinese Jia-A League</a> and the later rebranded <a href="/wiki/Chinese_Super_League" title="Chinese Super League">Chinese Super League</a>, and was widely considered one of the most successful clubs in Chinese football history.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Shide_74-0"><a href="#cite_note-Shide-74">[74]</a></sup> In the <a href="/wiki/Asian_Football_Confederation" title="Asian Football Confederation">Asian Football Confederation</a>, the club reached the <a href="/wiki/1997%E2%80%9398_Asian_Club_Championship" title="1997–98 Asian Club Championship">1997–98 Asian Club Championship</a> and <a href="/wiki/2000%E2%80%9301_Asian_Cup_Winners%27_Cup" title="2000–01 Asian Cup Winners' Cup">2000–01 Asian Cup Winners' Cup</a> finals. Several of China’s greatest players, including <a href="/wiki/Sun_Jihai" title="Sun Jihai">Sun Jihai</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hao_Haidong" title="Hao Haidong">Hao Haidong</a> and <a href="/wiki/Li_Ming_(footballer,_born_1971)" title="Li Ming (footballer, born 1971)">Li Ming</a>, made their names with <a href="/wiki/Dalian_Shide_F.C." title="Dalian Shide F.C.">Dalian Shide</a>. Dalian also produced many top Chinese football players thanks to its youth training system and grassroots football culture.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-football_culture_75-0"><a href="#cite_note-football_culture-75">[75]</a></sup> As of the <a href="/wiki/2014_Chinese_Super_League" title="2014 Chinese Super League">2014 season</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Chinese_Super_League" title="Chinese Super League">Chinese Super League</a>, out of the 448 registered Chinese players, a total of 71 players are from Dalian.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-football_culture_75-1"><a href="#cite_note-football_culture-75">[75]</a></sup> Therefore, Dalian earned its nickname of China's "Football City" (<span lang="zh-Hans">足球城</span>),<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-76"><a href="#cite_note-76">[76]</a></sup> and a giant football statue was placed in the Labor Park near downtown Dalian in its honor. Current football clubs in the city are <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Dalian_Yifang" title="Dalian Yifang">Dalian Yifang</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Dalian_Transcendence" title="Dalian Transcendence">Dalian Transcendence</a>, which play in the country's 2nd-tier league, the <a href="/wiki/China_League_One" title="China League One">China League One</a>. Their home stadiums are <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Dalian_Sports_Center" title="Dalian Sports Center">Dalian Sports Center Stadium</a> and <a href="/wiki/Jinzhou_Stadium" title="Jinzhou Stadium">Jinzhou Stadium</a>, respectively.</p>
<p>Some other popular sports played in Dalian are swimming, skiing, golf, cycling, bowling and billiards.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (February 2014)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></p>
<p>As part of the <a href="/wiki/2013_National_Games_of_China" title="2013 National Games of China">2013 National Games of China</a> in <a href="/wiki/Liaoning" title="Liaoning">Liaoning</a> in 2013, Dalian was a host city for 12 events, including <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Synchronized_swimming" title="Synchronized swimming">synchronized swimming</a>, <a href="/wiki/Field_hockey" title="Field hockey">field hockey</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gymnastics" title="Gymnastics">gymnastics</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sailing" title="Sailing">sailing</a> and <a href="/wiki/Canoeing" title="Canoeing">canoeing</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-77"><a href="#cite_note-77">[77]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="City-wide_festivals_and_events">City-wide festivals and events</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Dalian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: City-wide festivals and events">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:%E6%BB%A8%E6%B5%B7%E4%B8%AD%E8%B7%AF%E7%BA%A65000%E7%B1%B3(retouched).jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1872" data-file-width="3328" height="124" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/42/%E6%BB%A8%E6%B5%B7%E4%B8%AD%E8%B7%AF%E7%BA%A65000%E7%B1%B3%28retouched%29.jpg/220px-%E6%BB%A8%E6%B5%B7%E4%B8%AD%E8%B7%AF%E7%BA%A65000%E7%B1%B3%28retouched%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/42/%E6%BB%A8%E6%B5%B7%E4%B8%AD%E8%B7%AF%E7%BA%A65000%E7%B1%B3%28retouched%29.jpg/330px-%E6%BB%A8%E6%B5%B7%E4%B8%AD%E8%B7%AF%E7%BA%A65000%E7%B1%B3%28retouched%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/42/%E6%BB%A8%E6%B5%B7%E4%B8%AD%E8%B7%AF%E7%BA%A65000%E7%B1%B3%28retouched%29.jpg/440px-%E6%BB%A8%E6%B5%B7%E4%B8%AD%E8%B7%AF%E7%BA%A65000%E7%B1%B3%28retouched%29.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:%E6%BB%A8%E6%B5%B7%E4%B8%AD%E8%B7%AF%E7%BA%A65000%E7%B1%B3(retouched).jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Binhai Road is the main route for Dalian International Walking Festival. View of mountain on one side and sea on the other makes it a popular exercise destination for local people.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p><a href="/wiki/Xinghai_Square" title="Xinghai Square">Xinghai Square</a>, Dalian Xinghai Convention &amp; Exhibitions Center, the Dalian World Expo Center and the hotels on Renmin Road are the main places where Dalian's major annual events are held.</p>
<p>Every year from January to February, the Bingyugou Ice Lantern Festival is held in Bingyugou Scenic Area in <a href="/wiki/Zhuanghe" title="Zhuanghe">Zhuanghe City</a>. The event features a large number of ice sculptures, snow sculptures and colorful ice lanterns. Visitors can also participate in a series of ice-sports including ice-skating, ice hockey and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Iceboating" title="Iceboating">iceboating</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-78"><a href="#cite_note-78">[78]</a></sup></p>
<p>From late April to May, the Lüshun International Cherry Blossom Festival is held. The main site is <a href="/wiki/203_Hill" title="203 Hill">203 Hill</a>, and the other site is <a href="/wiki/Longwangtang_Cherry_Blossom_Park" title="Longwangtang Cherry Blossom Park">Longwangtang Cherry Blossom Park</a>. It is said that the very first cherry trees were planted by Japanese soldiers stationed in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/L%C3%BCshun" title="Lüshun">Lüshun</a> during <a href="/wiki/World_War_II" title="World War II">World War II</a>, in order to ease their homesickness. Today, the 203 Hill site has more than 3000 cherry trees, and boasts to be the largest <a href="/wiki/Cherry_blossom" title="Cherry blossom">cherry blossom</a> park in China with the most varieties.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-79"><a href="#cite_note-79">[79]</a></sup></p>
<p>Each May, the Dalian International Walking Festival takes place. The purpose of the festival is to foster health and peace for the whole community. It is widely popular among citizens and attracts many foreign participants. Dalian is the only city in China recognized by the <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=IML_Walking_Association&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="IML Walking Association (page does not exist)">IML Walking Association</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-80"><a href="#cite_note-80">[80]</a></sup> Four different routes of 30 kilometres (19 miles), 20 kilometres (12 miles), 10 kilometres (6.2 miles) and 5 kilometres (3.1 miles) are provided for participants, with the longest route going from <a href="/wiki/Xinghai_Square" title="Xinghai Square">Xinghai Square</a> along Binhai Road to Laohutan Ocean Park, Bangchuidao Scenic Area and finally reaching Dalian International Conference Center. Starting from 2012, Jinshitan National Holiday Resort also serves as a venue for the festival.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-81"><a href="#cite_note-81">[81]</a></sup></p>
<p>Every May, <a href="/wiki/Dalian_International_Marathon" title="Dalian International Marathon">Dalian International Marathon</a> is held. With the first marathon held in 1987, it is one of the four oldest marathon races in China.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-82"><a href="#cite_note-82">[82]</a></sup> The main venue is the Jinshitan National Holiday Resort.</p>
<p>Every June, the China International Software &amp; Information Service Fair is held in Dalian World Expo Center. Officials from overseas government departments, CEOs of World Top 500, well-known consulting firms and overseas IT associations attend the fair each year.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-83"><a href="#cite_note-83">[83]</a></sup></p>
<p>Dalian International Beer Festival takes place in <a href="/wiki/Xinghai_Square" title="Xinghai Square">Xinghai Square</a> every year from July to August. It is similar to <a href="/wiki/Oktoberfest" title="Oktoberfest">Oktoberfest</a> in <a href="/wiki/Munich" title="Munich">Munich</a> and is a widely popular event in the city. Activities of the Beer Festival include exhibitions by beer manufacturers, a beer disco plaza, a beer culture exhibition, a beer drinking contest, a photography contest, the Beer Industry Summit, and a beer quiz.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-84"><a href="#cite_note-84">[84]</a></sup></p>
<p>Dalian International Automotive Exhibition is held in August in Dalian Xinghai Convention &amp; Exhibitions Center and Dalian World Expo Center.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-85"><a href="#cite_note-85">[85]</a></sup></p>
<p>The annual Dalian International Fashion Festival is held in September in Dalian Xinghai Convention &amp; Exhibitions Center and Dalian World Expo Center. For the past decade, the festival has been attracting the world's top fashion designers, businessmen and models to Dalian. Arrangement for the show includes various theme activities including the Garment Export Fair, fashion exhibitions, fashion competitions and a model contest.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-86"><a href="#cite_note-86">[86]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Inter-governmental">Inter-governmental</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Dalian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Inter-governmental">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Japan maintains a branch office for its <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Consulate_General" title="Consulate General">Consulate General</a> of Japan at Shenyang and a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/JETRO" title="JETRO">JETRO</a> office in Dalian, reflecting a relatively large Japanese population.</p>
<p>Japan Chamber of Commerce &amp; Industry has about 700 corporate members.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (December 2015)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup> Those Japanese who had lived in Dalian before the War have organized the Dalian Society.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Religion">Religion</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Dalian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Religion">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tleft">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Lianhuashan_Temple.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3456" data-file-width="5184" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f6/Lianhuashan_Temple.jpg/220px-Lianhuashan_Temple.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f6/Lianhuashan_Temple.jpg/330px-Lianhuashan_Temple.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f6/Lianhuashan_Temple.jpg/440px-Lianhuashan_Temple.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Lianhuashan_Temple.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Lianhuashan (lit. "lotus flower mountain") Temple, Dalian</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>As of 2005<sup class="plainlinks noprint asof-tag update" style="display:none;"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Dalian&amp;action=edit">[update]</a></sup>, Dalian had 29 Christian churches (27 of them Protestant, 2 of them Catholic), 10 mosques, 34 Buddhist temples, and 7 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Taoist" title="Taoist">Taoist</a> temples, according to the statistics of the city government.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-MZW_87-0"><a href="#cite_note-MZW-87">[87]</a></sup></p>
<p>Taoist temples can be found in various districts including downtown Dalian (Hua Temple in Zhongshan Park), in Lüshunkou District (Longwang Temple), and in Jinzhou District (Jinlong Temple in Daweijia, Xiangshui Temple at the foot of <a href="/wiki/Dahei_Mountain" title="Dahei Mountain">Dahei Mountain</a>, and Zhenwu Temple in Liangjiadian).</p>
<p>Buddhist temples are in downtown Dalian (Songshan Temple on Tangshan Street and Lianhuashan Temple on Yingchun Road), on the northern side of Anzi Mountain (Anshan Temple), at Daheishi (Thousand-Hand Buddha &amp; 500 Luohan Statues), in Lüshunkou District (Hengshan Temple at Longwangtang), and in Jinzhou District (Guanyinge-Shengshui Temple on Dahei Mountain).</p>
<p><a href="/wiki/Dalian_Catholic_Church" title="Dalian Catholic Church">Dalian Catholic Church</a> (built in 1926) is in downtown Dalian, west of Dalian Railway Station. Protestant churches are near Zhongshan Square (<a href="/wiki/Yuguang_Street_Church" title="Yuguang Street Church">Yuguang Street Church</a>, the former <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Dalian_Anglican_Church" title="Dalian Anglican Church">Dalian Anglican Church</a>, built in 1928 in the British Consulate General's premises by the <a href="/wiki/Church_of_England" title="Church of England">Church of England</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Nippon_Sei_Ko_Kai" title="Nippon Sei Ko Kai">Anglican Church of Japan</a> jointly), on Changjiang Road (<a href="/wiki/Beijing_Street_Church" title="Beijing Street Church">Beijing Street Church</a>, now called Cheng-en Church, originally built in 1914 by the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Danish_National_Church" title="Danish National Church">Danish Lutheran Church</a>), on Xi'an Road (Christian Church for Korean Chinese and South Koreans), east of the airport (the newly built Harvest Church, which can seat 4000 people), in Jinzhou (the newly built Jinzhou Church) and in Lüshunkou District (Lüshun Church, a former Danish Lutheran church). <a href="/wiki/Dalian_Mosque" title="Dalian Mosque">Dalian Mosque</a> is on Beijing Street.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-MZW_87-1"><a href="#cite_note-MZW-87">[87]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Notable_people">Notable people</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Dalian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Notable people">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Liu_Changchun.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2848" data-file-width="4272" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/55/Liu_Changchun.jpg/220px-Liu_Changchun.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/55/Liu_Changchun.jpg/330px-Liu_Changchun.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/55/Liu_Changchun.jpg/440px-Liu_Changchun.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Liu_Changchun.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<a href="/wiki/Liu_Changchun" title="Liu Changchun">Liu Changchun</a> statue at Olympic Square, Dalian</div>
</div>
</div>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bo_Xilai" title="Bo Xilai">Bo Xilai</a> (薄熙来), former mayor, removed from Politburo under corruption charges.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Liu_Changchun" title="Liu Changchun">Liu Changchun</a> (刘长春), <a href="/wiki/Sprint_(running)" title="Sprint (running)">sprinter</a>, first athlete to represent China in competition at the Olympic Games.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Dong_Jie" title="Dong Jie">Dong Jie</a> (董洁), actress.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Yu_Nan" title="Yu Nan">Yu Nan</a> (余男), actress.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Xia_Deren" title="Xia Deren">Xia Deren</a> (夏德仁), former mayor from October 2006 to May 2009.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-88"><a href="#cite_note-88">[88]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-89"><a href="#cite_note-89">[89]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Xue_Jiye" title="Xue Jiye">Xue Jiye</a> (薛继业), painter and sculptor.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bi_Fujian" title="Bi Fujian">Bi Fujian</a> (毕福剑), director, host and professor.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Lou_Yixiao" title="Lou Yixiao">Lou Yixiao</a> (娄艺潇), actress.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Sun_Nan" title="Sun Nan">Sun Nan</a> (孙楠), singer.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Sun_Jihai" title="Sun Jihai">Sun Jihai</a> (孙继海), footballer.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Lin_Peng" title="Lin Peng">Lin Peng</a> (林鹏), actress.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Li_Yongbo" title="Li Yongbo">Li Yongbo</a> (李永波), retired badminton player and current head coach of the <a href="/wiki/China_national_badminton_team" title="China national badminton team">China National Badminton Team</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Lai_Yawen" title="Lai Yawen">Lai Yawen</a> (赖亚文), retired middle blocker and current assistant coach of the <a href="/wiki/China_women%27s_national_volleyball_team" title="China women's national volleyball team">China women's national volleyball team</a>.</li>
</ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Education">Education</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Dalian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Education">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>There were 23 general institutions of higher education (and another 7 privately run colleges), 108 secondary vocational schools, 80 ordinary middle high schools, 1,049 schools for nine-year compulsory education and 1,432 kindergartens in Dalian. The students on campus of all levels (including kindergartens) totaled 1108 thousand.</p>
<p>There are the following schools of higher education and research centres:</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Colleges_and_universities">Colleges and universities</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Dalian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: Colleges and universities">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Dalian_University_of_Technology" title="Dalian University of Technology">Dalian University of Technology</a> (大连理工大学)（<a href="/wiki/Project_985" title="Project 985">Project 985</a>, <a href="/wiki/Project_211" title="Project 211">Project 211</a>）</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Dalian_Maritime_University" title="Dalian Maritime University">Dalian Maritime University</a> (大连海事大学)（<a href="/wiki/Project_211" title="Project 211">Project 211</a>）</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Dongbei_University_of_Finance_and_Economics" title="Dongbei University of Finance and Economics">Dongbei University of Finance and Economics</a> (东北财经大学)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Dalian_Jiaotong_University" title="Dalian Jiaotong University">Dalian Jiaotong University</a> (大连交通大学) (Founded in 1956)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Dalian_University_of_Foreign_Languages" title="Dalian University of Foreign Languages">Dalian University of Foreign Languages</a> (大连外国语大学)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Liaoning_Normal_University" title="Liaoning Normal University">Liaoning Normal University</a> (辽宁师范大学)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Dalian_Medical_University" title="Dalian Medical University">Dalian Medical University</a> (大连医科大学) (Founded in 1947)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Dalian_University" title="Dalian University">Dalian University</a> (大连大学)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Dalian_Nationalities_University" title="Dalian Nationalities University">Dalian Nationalities University</a> (大连民族大学) (Founded in 1997)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Dalian_Naval_Academy" title="Dalian Naval Academy">Dalian Naval Academy</a> of the <a href="/wiki/People%27s_Liberation_Army_Navy" title="People's Liberation Army Navy">PLA Navy</a>（中国人民解放军海军大连舰艇学院）</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Dalian_Ocean_University" title="Dalian Ocean University">Dalian Ocean University</a> (大连海洋大学) (Founded in 1952)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Dalian_Polytechnic_University" title="Dalian Polytechnic University">Dalian Polytechnic University</a> (大连工业大学)</li>

</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Research_centres">Research centres</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Dalian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: Research centres">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Dalian_Institute_of_Chemical_Physics" title="Dalian Institute of Chemical Physics">Dalian Institute of Chemical Physics</a> (<a class="extiw" href="https://zh.wikipedia.org/wiki/%E4%B8%AD%E5%9B%BD%E7%A7%91%E5%AD%A6%E9%99%A2%E5%A4%A7%E8%BF%9E%E5%8C%96%E5%AD%A6%E7%89%A9%E7%90%86%E7%A0%94%E7%A9%B6%E6%89%80" title="zh:中国科学院大连化学物理研究所">大连化学物理研究所</a> or 化物所), of the <a href="/wiki/Chinese_Academy_of_Sciences" title="Chinese Academy of Sciences">Chinese Academy of Sciences</a> (中国科学院)</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="High_schools">High schools</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Dalian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=41" title="Edit section: High schools">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Notable high schools include:</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Dalian_No._24_High_School" title="Dalian No. 24 High School">Dalian No. 24 High School</a> (大连市第二十四中学)</li>
<li><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Dalian_Yuming_Senior_High_School&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Dalian Yuming Senior High School (page does not exist)">Dalian Yuming Senior High School</a> (大连育明高级中学)</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Dalian_No._8_High_School" title="Dalian No. 8 High School">Dalian No. 8 High School</a> (<a class="extiw" href="https://zh.wikipedia.org/wiki/%E5%A4%A7%E8%BF%9E%E5%B8%82%E7%AC%AC%E5%85%AB%E4%B8%AD%E5%AD%A6" title="zh:大连市第八中学">大连市第八中学</a>)</li>
<li><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Dalian_No._1_High_School&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Dalian No. 1 High School (page does not exist)">Dalian No. 1 High School</a> (大连市第一中学), Founded in 1922 by Japanese. It was the first school institute in Dalian.</li>
<li><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Dalian_No._12_High_School&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Dalian No. 12 High School (page does not exist)">Dalian No. 12 High School</a> (大连市第十二中学)</li>
<li><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Dalian_No._36_High_School&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Dalian No. 36 High School (page does not exist)">Dalian No. 36 High School</a> (大连市第三十六中学)</li>
<li><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=The_High_School_Affiliated_to_Liaoning_Normal_University&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="The High School Affiliated to Liaoning Normal University (page does not exist)">The High School Affiliated to Liaoning Normal University</a> (辽宁师范大学附属中学)</li>
<li><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=The_High_School_Attached_to_Dalian_University_of_Technology&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="The High School Attached to Dalian University of Technology (page does not exist)">The High School Attached to Dalian University of Technology</a> (<a class="extiw" href="https://zh.wikipedia.org/wiki/%E5%A4%A7%E8%BF%9E%E7%90%86%E5%B7%A5%E5%A4%A7%E5%AD%A6%E9%99%84%E5%B1%9E%E9%AB%98%E4%B8%AD" title="zh:大连理工大学附属高中">大连理工大学附属高中</a>)</li>
<li><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Dalian_L%C3%BCshun_Senior_High_School&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Dalian Lüshun Senior High School (page does not exist)">Dalian Lüshun Senior High School</a> (大连市旅顺中学)</li>
<li><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Dalian_Jinzhou_Senior_High_School&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Dalian Jinzhou Senior High School (page does not exist)">Dalian Jinzhou Senior High School</a>（大连市金州高级中学）</li>
</ul>

<p>Since 29 April 2008, Dalian has had a friendship city agreement with <a href="/wiki/Dallas" title="Dallas">Dallas</a>, United States.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-95"><a href="#cite_note-95">[95]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Dallas_sisters_96-0"><a href="#cite_note-Dallas_sisters-96">[96]</a></sup></p>

<tr>

<table class="nowraplinks navbox-subgroup" style="border-spacing:0">
<tr>
<th class="navbox-group" scope="row" style="padding-left:0;padding-right:0;">
<div style="padding:0em 0.75em;"><a href="/wiki/Prefectures_of_the_People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="Prefectures of the People's Republic of China">Prefecture-level capitals</a><br/>
(County-level)</div>
</th>
<td class="navbox-list navbox-odd" style="text-align:left;border-left-width:2px;border-left-style:solid;width:100%;padding:0px">
<div style="padding:0em 0.25em">
<ul>
<li>(<a href="/wiki/Inner_Mongolia" title="Inner Mongolia">Inner Mongolia</a>: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ulanhot" title="Ulanhot">Ulanhot</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Xilinhot" title="Xilinhot">Xilinhot</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jiagedaqi_District" title="Jiagedaqi District">Jiagedaqi</a><sup>3</sup>, <a href="/wiki/Heilongjiang" title="Heilongjiang">Heilongjiang</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Enshi_City" title="Enshi City">Enshi</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hubei" title="Hubei">Hubei</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jishou" title="Jishou">Jishou</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hunan" title="Hunan">Hunan</a></li>
<li>(<a href="/wiki/Sichuan" title="Sichuan">Sichuan</a>：<a href="/wiki/Xichang" title="Xichang">Xichang</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Kangding" title="Kangding">Kangding</a></li>

<tr>
<td class="navbox-list navbox-odd" colspan="2" style="width:100%;padding:0px">
<div style="padding:0em 0.25em">* Indicates this city has already occurred above.<br/>
<p><sup>a</sup><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Direct-controlled_municipality_of_China" title="Direct-controlled municipality of China">Direct-controlled Municipalities</a>. <sup>b</sup><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sub-provincial_city_in_the_People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="Sub-provincial city in the People's Republic of China">Sub-provincial cities as provincial capitals</a>. <sup>c</sup><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sub-provincial_city_in_the_People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="Sub-provincial city in the People's Republic of China">Separate state-planning cities</a>. <sup>1</sup><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Special_Economic_Zones_of_China" title="Special Economic Zones of China">Special Economic Zone Cities</a>. <sup>2</sup><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Special_Economic_Zones_of_China" title="Special Economic Zones of China">Coastal development cities</a>.<br/>
<sup>3</sup>Prefecture capital status established by Heilongjiang Province and not recognized by Ministry of Civil Affairs. Disputed by <a href="/wiki/Oroqen_Autonomous_Banner" title="Oroqen Autonomous Banner">Oroqen Autonomous Banner</a>, Hulunbuir, Inner Mongolia as part of it.<br/>
<sup>4</sup>Only administers islands and waters in South China Sea and have no urban core comparable to typical cities in China.<br/>
<sup>5</sup>The claimed province of <a href="/wiki/Taiwan_Province,_People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="Taiwan Province, People's Republic of China">Taiwan</a> no longer have any internal division announced by Ministry of Civil Affairs of PRC, due to lack of actual jurisdiction. See <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Template:Administrative_divisions_of_the_Republic_of_China" title="Template:Administrative divisions of the Republic of China">Template:Administrative divisions of the Republic of China</a> instead.<br/></p>
All provincial capitals are listed first in prefecture-level cities by province.</div>
